rerework_investment.101 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = imperialist_investments_events.4.t
	desc = rerework_investments_events.4.d.1
	flavor = imperialist_investments_events.4.fx

	event_image = {
		video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"

	duration = 1
	
	option = {
		name = imperialist_investments_events.4.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = tgr_investment_will_be_conducted_tooltip
			scope:scope_rootxxx = {
				trigger_event = { id = rerework_investments.201 }
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:scope_rootxxx
			value = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = imperialist_investments_events.4.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = tgr_investment_will_not_be_conducted_tooltip
			scope:scope_rootxxx = {
				trigger_event = { id = rerework_investment.401 }
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:scope_rootxxx
			value = -5
		}
	}
}

rerework_investments.201 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = imperialist_investments_events.4.tx
	desc = rerework_investments_events.4.dx.1
	flavor = imperialist_investments_events.4.f

	event_image = {
		video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"

	duration = 1
	
	option = {
		name = imperialist_investments_events.4.ax
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = tgr_investment_will_be_conducted_1_tooltip
			trigger_event = { id = imperialist_investments.211 weeks = 23 }
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = very_high_investment_modifier
			weeks = 23
		}
	}
}

rerework_investments.301 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		exists = scope:target_country
		exists = scope:economic_investment_chosen_state
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
					NOT = {
						has_building = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
					}
				}
			}
			scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
				create_building = {
					building = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
				create_building = {
					building = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
					level = 2
				}
			}
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
						level = 2
					}
				}
			}
			scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
				create_building = {
					building = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
					level = 3
				}
			}
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_hydroelectric_power_plant
						level = 3
					}
				}
			}
			scope:economic_investment_chosen_state = {
				create_building = {
					building = building_hydroelectric_power_plant

				}
